    16	package org.openrewrite.maven;

    19	import lombok.Value;
    20	import org.jspecify.annotations.Nullable;

    27	import org.openrewrite.xml.ChangeTagValueVisitor;
    28	import org.openrewrite.xml.tree.Xml;

    30	import java.util.Objects;
    31	import java.util.Optional;
    32	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    33	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    34	
    35	import static org.openrewrite.internal.StringUtils.isNullOrEmpty;
    36	
    37	@Value
    38	@EqualsAndHashCode(callSuper = false)
    39	public class UpdateScmFromGitOrigin extends Recipe {
    40	
    41	    @Option(displayName = "Add if missing",
    42	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will add a `<scm>` section if it is missing. " +
    43	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will only update existing `<scm>` sections.",
    44	            required = false)
    45	    @Nullable
    46	    Boolean addIfMissing;
    47	
    48	    String displayName = "Update SCM with Git origin";
    49	
    50	    String description = "Updates or adds the Maven `<scm>` tag based on the Git remote origin. " +
    51	               "By default, only existing Source Control Management (SCM) sections are updated. Set `addIfMissing` to `true` to also add missing SCM sections.";
    52	
    53	    @Override
    54	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
    55	        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
    56	
    57	            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
    58	            GitOrigin gitOrigin;
    59	
    60	            @Override
    61	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    62	                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
    63	                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
    64	                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
    65	                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
    66	                    return document;
    67	                }
    68	                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();
    69	
    70	                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
    71	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
    72	                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
    73	                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
    74	                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
    75	                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
    76	                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
    77	                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
    78	                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
    79	                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
    80	                                "</scm>";
    81	                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
    82	                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
    83	                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));
    84	
    85	                    }
    86	                    return document;
    87	                }
    88	
    89	                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
    90	            }
    91	
    92	            @Override
    93	            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    94	                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
    95	                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
    96	                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
    97	                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
    98	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
    99	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
   100	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
   101	                }
   102	                return tag;
   103	            }
   104	
   105	            private Xml.Tag updateScmTag(Xml.Tag tag, String tagName, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   106	                Optional<Xml.Tag> maybeChild = tag.getChild(tagName);
   107	                if (maybeChild.isPresent()) {
   108	                    Xml.Tag childTag = maybeChild.get();
   109	                    String originalUrl = childTag.getValue().orElse("");
   110	                    String updatedUrl = gitOrigin.replaceHostAndPath(originalUrl);
   111	                    if (!originalUrl.equals(updatedUrl)) {
   112	                        tag = (Xml.Tag) new ChangeTagValueVisitor<>(childTag, updatedUrl)
   113	                                .visitNonNull(tag, ctx, getCursor().getParentTreeCursor());
   114	                    }
   115	                }
   116	                return tag;
   117	            }
   118	        };
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    @Value
   122	    static class GitOrigin {
   123	        private static final Pattern[] URL_PATTERNS = {
   124	                // SSH format: git@host:path(.git)?
   125	                Pattern.compile("^git@([^:]+):(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   126	
   127	                // HTTP/HTTPS with optional username and port: http(s)://[username@]host[:port]/path(.git)?
   128	                Pattern.compile("^https?://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   129	
   130	                // SSH with protocol and port: ssh://git@host[:port]/path(.git)?
   131	                Pattern.compile("^ssh://git@([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   132	
   133	                // Generic protocol://[user@]host[:port]/path(.git)? - catches any other protocols
   134	                Pattern.compile("^[a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$")
   135	        };
   136	
   137	        String host;
   138	        String path;
   139	
   140	        static @Nullable GitOrigin parseGitUrl(String gitUrl) {
   141	            if (!isNullOrEmpty(gitUrl)) {
   142	                for (Pattern pattern : URL_PATTERNS) {
   143	                    Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(gitUrl);
   144	                    if (matcher.matches()) {
   145	                        return new GitOrigin(matcher.group(1), matcher.group(2));
   146	                    }
   147	                }
   148	            }
   149	            return null;
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        String replaceHostAndPath(String originalUrl) {
   153	            if (isNullOrEmpty(originalUrl)) {
   154	                return originalUrl;
   155	            }
   156	
   157	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("scm:git:")) {
   158	                String actualUrl = originalUrl.substring("scm:git:".length());
   159	                return "scm:git:" + replaceHostAndPath(actualUrl);
   160	            }
   161	
   162	            // Handle git@ format (SSH)
   163	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("git@")) {
   164	                // First check if the URL already has the correct host and path
   165	                String expectedPrefix = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   166	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
   167	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, don't modify
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                // Otherwise, replace the host and path
   171	                Matcher gitMatcher = Pattern.compile("^git@[^:]+:(.+?)$").matcher(originalUrl);
   172	                if (gitMatcher.matches()) {
   173	                    String originalFullPath = gitMatcher.group(1);
   174	                    // Check if original path ends with .git
   175	                    boolean hasGitExtension = originalFullPath.endsWith(".git");
   176	
   177	                    // Build new URL
   178	                    String newUrl = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   179	                    if (hasGitExtension && !path.endsWith(".git")) {
   180	                        newUrl += ".git";
   181	                    }
   182	                    return newUrl;
   183	                }
   184	            }
   185	
   186	            // Handle protocol-based URLs (http, https, ssh, etc.)
   187	            Matcher protocolMatcher = Pattern.compile("^([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://)(?:([^@/]+)@)?([^/]+)(/[^?#]*)?(.*)?$").matcher(originalUrl);
   188	            if (protocolMatcher.find()) {
   189	                String protocol = protocolMatcher.group(1);
   190	                String user = protocolMatcher.group(2);
   191	                String originalHost = protocolMatcher.group(3);
   192	                String originalPath = protocolMatcher.group(4);
   193	                String suffix = protocolMatcher.group(5) != null ? protocolMatcher.group(5) : "";
   194	
   195	                String userPrefix = (user != null) ? user + "@" : "";
   196	
   197	                // Determine if we need to add .git extension
   198	                boolean needsGitExtension = originalPath != null && originalPath.endsWith(".git") && !path.endsWith(".git");
   199	                String newPath = "/" + path + (needsGitExtension ? ".git" : "");
   200	
   201	                // Check if the base URL already matches (to preserve suffixes)
   202	                String newBaseUrl = protocol + userPrefix + host + newPath;
   203	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(newBaseUrl)) {
   204	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, preserve any suffix
   205	                }
   206	
   207	                return newBaseUrl + suffix;
   208	            }
   209	
   210	            // Return the original URL if no patterns matched
   211	            return originalUrl;
   212	        }
   213	    }

    96	    public @Nullable ResolvedDependency getResolvedDependency(Dependency dependency) {
    97	        for (int i = Scope.values().length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    98	            Scope scope = Scope.values()[i];
    99	            if (dependencies.containsKey(scope)) {
   100	                for (ResolvedDependency resolvedDependency : dependencies.get(scope)) {
   101	                    if (resolvedDependency.getRequested() == dependency) {
   102	                        return resolvedDependency;
   103	                    }
   104	                }
   105	            }
   106	        }
   107	        return null;
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    /**
   111	     * Finds dependencies (including any transitive dependencies) in the model that match the provided group and
   112	     * artifact ids. The search can optionally be limited to a given scope.
   113	     * <p>
   114	     * Note: It is possible for the same dependency to be returned multiple times if it is present in multiple scopes.
   115	     *
   116	     * @param groupId    The groupId as a glob expression
   117	     * @param artifactId The artifactId as a glob expression
   118	     * @param scope      The scope to limit the search to, or null to search all scopes
   119	     * @return A list of matching dependencies
   120	     */
   121	    public List<ResolvedDependency> findDependencies(String groupId, String artifactId, @Nullable Scope scope) {
   122	        return findDependencies(d -> matchesGlob(d.getGroupId(), groupId) && matchesGlob(d.getArtifactId(), artifactId), scope);
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    /**
   126	     * Finds dependencies (including any transitive dependencies) in the model that match the predicate. The search can
   127	     * optionally be limited to a given scope.
   128	     * <p>
   129	     * Note: It is possible for the same dependency to be returned multiple times if it is present in multiple scopes.
   130	     *
   131	     * @param matcher The predicate to match the dependency
   132	     * @param scope   A scope to limit the search to, or null to search all scopes
   133	     * @return A list of matching dependencies
   134	     */
   135	    public List<ResolvedDependency> findDependencies(Predicate<ResolvedDependency> matcher, @Nullable Scope scope) {
   136	        List<ResolvedDependency> found = null;
   137	        for (Map.Entry<Scope, List<ResolvedDependency>> entry : dependencies.entrySet()) {
   138	            if (scope != null && entry.getKey() != scope) {
   139	                continue;
   140	            }
   141	
   142	            for (ResolvedDependency d : entry.getValue()) {
   143	                if (matcher.test(d)) {
   144	                    if (found == null) {
   145	                        found = new ArrayList<>();
   146	                    }
   147	                    found.add(d);
   148	                }
   149	            }
   150	        }
   151	        return found == null ? emptyList() : found;
   152	    }

   173	        for (ResolvedManagedDependency dm : pom.getDependencyManagement()) {
   174	            if (dm.getRequested() == dependency || dm.getRequestedBom() == dependency) {
   175	                return dm;
   176	            }
   177	        }
   178	        return null;
   179	    }

   181	    private static final Scope[] RESOLVE_SCOPES = new Scope[]{Scope.Compile, Scope.Runtime, Scope.Test, Scope.Provided};
   182	
   183	    public MavenResolutionResult resolveDependencies(MavenPomDownloader downloader, ExecutionContext ctx) throws MavenDownloadingExceptions {
   184	        Map<Scope, List<ResolvedDependency>> dependencies = new LinkedHashMap<>();
   185	        MavenDownloadingExceptions exceptions = null;
   186	
   187	        Map<GroupArtifact, Set<GroupArtifactVersion>> exceptionsInLowerScopes = new HashMap<>();
   188	        for (Scope scope : RESOLVE_SCOPES) {
   189	            try {
   190	                dependencies.put(scope, pom.resolveDependencies(scope, downloader, ctx));
   191	            } catch (MavenDownloadingExceptions e) {
   192	                for (MavenDownloadingException exception : e.getExceptions()) {
   193	                    if (exceptionsInLowerScopes.computeIfAbsent(new GroupArtifact(
   194	                            exception.getRoot().getGroupId() == null ? "" : exception.getRoot().getGroupId(),
   195	                            exception.getRoot().getArtifactId()), ga -> new HashSet<>()).add(exception.getFailedOn())) {
   196	                        exceptions = MavenDownloadingExceptions.append(exceptions, exception);
   197	                    }
   198	                }
   199	            } catch (IllegalStateException e) {
   200	                throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to resolve dependencies of " + pom.getGav(), e);
   201	            }
   202	        }
   203	        if (exceptions != null) {
   204	            throw exceptions;
   205	        }
   206	        return withDependencies(dependencies);
   207	    }
   208	
   209	    public Map<Path, Pom> getProjectPoms() {
   210	        Map<Path, Pom> projectPoms = new HashMap<>();
   211	        getProjectPomsRecursive(projectPoms);
   212	        return projectPoms;
   213	    }
   214	
   215	    /**
   216	     * Often recipes operating on multi-module projects will prefer to make changes to the parent pom rather than in multiple child poms.
   217	     * But if the parent isn't in the same repository as the child, the recipe would need to be applied to the child poms.
   218	     *
   219	     * @return true when the parent pom of the current pom is present in the same repository as the current pom
   220	     */
   221	    public boolean parentPomIsProjectPom() {
   222	        if (getParent() == null) {
   223	            return false;
   224	        }
   225	        ResolvedGroupArtifactVersion parentGav = getParent().getPom().getGav();
   226	        return getProjectPoms().values().stream()
   227	                .map(Pom::getGav)
   228	                .anyMatch(gav -> gav.equals(parentGav));
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    public boolean isMultiModulePom() {
   232	        return getPom().getSubprojects() == null || !getPom().getSubprojects().isEmpty();
   233	    }
   234	
   235	    private void getProjectPomsRecursive(Map<Path, Pom> projectPoms) {
   236	        // Strange edge case: Some projects specify a <relativePath> to their parent in the maven local directory
   237	        // e.g.: ../../../.m2/repository/
   238	        // This is bizarre and generally pointless, but not technically disallowed by Maven
   239	        if (parent != null && !projectPoms.containsKey(parent.getPom().getRequested().getSourcePath())) {
   240	            Path parentPath = parent.getPom().getRequested().getSourcePath();
   241	            if (parentPath != null && !parentPath.toString().contains(".m2")) {
   242	                parent.getProjectPomsRecursive(projectPoms);
   243	            }
   244	        }
   245	        Path currentPath = requireNonNull(pom.getRequested().getSourcePath());
   246	        if (!currentPath.toString().contains(".m2")) {
   247	            projectPoms.put(currentPath, pom.getRequested());
   248	        }
   249	        for (MavenResolutionResult module : modules) {
   250	            if (!projectPoms.containsKey(module.getPom().getRequested().getSourcePath())) {
   251	                module.getProjectPomsRecursive(projectPoms);
   252	            }
   253	        }
   254	    }
   255	}

   182	    public static class Scanned {
   183	        boolean usingType;
   184	        List<SourceFile> rootPoms = new ArrayList<>();
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    @Override
   188	    public Scanned getInitialValue(ExecutionContext ctx) {
   189	        Scanned scanned = new Scanned();
   190	        scanned.usingType = onlyIfUsing == null;
   191	        return scanned;
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    @Override
   195	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getScanner(Scanned acc) {
   196	        return Preconditions.check(acc.usingType || (!StringUtils.isNullOrEmpty(onlyIfUsing) && onlyIfUsing.contains(":")), new MavenIsoVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
   197	            @Override
   198	            public Xml.Document visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   199	                document.getMarkers().findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class).ifPresent(mavenResolutionResult -> {
   200	                    if (mavenResolutionResult.getParent() == null) {
   201	                        acc.rootPoms.add(document);
   202	                    }
   203	                });
   204	                if (acc.usingType) {
   205	                    return document;
   206	                }
   207	                super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   208	                return document;
   209	            }
   210	
   211	            @Override
   212	            public Xml.Tag visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   213	                Xml.Tag t = super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
   214	
   215	                if (isDependencyTag()) {
   216	                    ResolvedDependency dependency = findDependency(t, null);
   217	                    if (dependency != null) {
   218	                        String[] ga = requireNonNull(onlyIfUsing).split(":");
   219	                        ResolvedDependency match = dependency.findDependency(ga[0], ga[1]);
   220	                        if (match != null) {
   221	                            acc.usingType = true;
   222	                        }
   223	                    }
   224	                }
   225	
   226	                return t;
   227	            }
   228	        });
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    @Override
   232	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor(Scanned acc) {
   233	        return Preconditions.check(acc.usingType, new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
   234	            @Override
   235	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   236	                Xml maven = super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   237	
   238	                if (!Boolean.TRUE.equals(addToRootPom) || acc.rootPoms.contains(document)) {
   239	                    ResolvedPom pom = getResolutionResult().getPom();
   240	                    String convertedVersion = pom.getValue(version);
   241	                    if (convertedVersion == null) {
   242	                        return maven;
   243	                    }
   244	                    String convertedGroup = requireNonNull(pom.getValue(groupId));
   245	                    String convertedArtifact = requireNonNull(pom.getValue(artifactId));
   246	                    Validated<VersionComparator> versionValidation = Semver.validate(convertedVersion, versionPattern);
   247	                    if (versionValidation.isValid()) {
   248	                        VersionComparator versionComparator = requireNonNull(versionValidation.getValue());
   249	                        try {
   250	                            // The version of the dependency currently in use (if any) might influence the version comparator
   251	                            // For example, "latest.patch" gives very different results depending on the version in use
   252	                            String currentVersion = getResolutionResult().findDependencies(convertedGroup, convertedArtifact, Scope.fromName(scope)).stream()
   253	                                    .map(ResolvedDependency::getVersion)
   254	                                    .findFirst()
   255	                                    .orElse(existingManagedDependencyVersion());
   256	                            String versionToUse = MavenDependency.findNewerVersion(convertedGroup, convertedArtifact, currentVersion, getResolutionResult(), metadataFailures, versionComparator, ctx);
   257	
   258	                            // Prevent downgrades
   259	                            if (currentVersion != null && versionToUse != null &&
   260	                                    versionComparator.compare(null, currentVersion, versionToUse) >= 0) {
   261	                                return maven;
   262	                            }
   263	
   264	                            if (versionToUse != null && !versionToUse.equals(pom.getValue(existingManagedDependencyVersion()))) {
   265	                                if (ResolvedPom.placeholderHelper.hasPlaceholders(version) && Objects.equals(convertedVersion, versionToUse)) {
   266	                                    // revert back to the original version if the version has a placeholder
   267	                                    versionToUse = version;
   268	                                }
   269	                                doAfterVisit(new AddManagedDependencyVisitor(groupId, artifactId,
   270	                                        versionToUse, scope, type, classifier, because));

    37	public class MavenVisitor<P> extends XmlVisitor<P> {
    38	
    39	    static final XPathMatcher DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/dependencies/dependency");
    40	    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/dependencies/dependency");
    41	    static final XPathMatcher PLUGIN_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//plugins/plugin/dependencies/dependency");
    42	    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_PLUGIN_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/build/plugins/plugin/dependencies/dependency");
    43	    static final XPathMatcher MANAGED_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/dependencyManagement/dependencies/dependency");
    44	    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_MANAGED_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/dependencyManagement/dependencies/dependency");
    45	    static final XPathMatcher PROPERTY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/properties/*");
    46	    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_PROPERTY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/properties/*");
    47	    static final XPathMatcher PLUGIN_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//plugins/plugin");
    48	    static final XPathMatcher ANNOTATION_PROCESSORS_PATH_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//annotationProcessorPaths/path");
    49	    static final XPathMatcher MANAGED_PLUGIN_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//pluginManagement/plugins/plugin");
    50	    static final XPathMatcher PARENT_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/parent");
    51	    static final XPathMatcher PROJECT_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project");
    52	
    53	    // there are several implicitly defined version properties that we should never attempt to update
    54	    private static final Set<String> IMPLICITLY_DEFINED_VERSION_PROPERTIES = new HashSet<>(Arrays.asList(
    55	            "${version}",
    56	            "${project.version}",
    57	            "${pom.version}",
    58	            "${project.parent.version}",
    59	            "${revision}",
    60	            "${sha1}",
    61	            "${changelist}"
    62	    ));
    63	
    64	    private transient Xml.@Nullable Document document;
    65	
    66	    @Nullable
    67	    private transient MavenResolutionResult resolutionResult;
    68	
    69	    @Override
    70	    public String getLanguage() {
    71	        return "maven";
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    @Override
    75	    public boolean isAcceptable(SourceFile sourceFile, P p) {
    76	        return super.isAcceptable(sourceFile, p) &&
    77	                sourceFile.getMarkers().findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class).isPresent();
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    protected MavenResolutionResult getResolutionResult() {
    81	        Iterator<Object> itr = getCursor()
    82	                .getPath(Xml.Document.class::isInstance);
    83	        if (itr.hasNext()) {
    84	            Xml.Document newDocument = (Xml.Document) itr.next();
    85	            if (document != null && document != newDocument) {
    86	                throw new IllegalStateException(
    87	                        "The same MavenVisitor instance has been used on two different XML documents. " +
    88	                                "This violates the Recipe contract that they will return a unique visitor instance every time getVisitor() is called.");
    89	            }
    90	            document = newDocument;
    91	        }
    92	        if (resolutionResult == null) {
    93	            resolutionResult = Optional.ofNullable(document)
    94	                    .map(Xml.Document::getMarkers)
    95	                    .flatMap(markers -> markers.findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class))
    96	                    .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Maven visitors should not be visiting XML documents without a Maven marker"));
    97	        }
    98	        return resolutionResult;
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    public boolean isPropertyTag() {
   102	        return PROPERTY_MATCHER.matches(getCursor());
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    public boolean isProfilePropertyTag() {
   106	        return PROFILE_PROPERTY_MATCHER.matches(getCursor());
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    public boolean isDependencyTag() {
   110	        return isTag("dependency") && DEPENDENCY_MATCHER.matches(getCursor());
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    /**
   114	     * Is a tag a dependency that matches the group and artifact?
   115	     *
   116	     * @param groupId    The group ID glob expression to compare the tag against.
   117	     * @param artifactId The artifact ID glob expression to compare the tag against.
   118	     * @return true if the tag matches.
   119	     */
   120	    public boolean isDependencyTag(String groupId, String artifactId) {
   121	        if (!isDependencyTag()) {
   122	            if (isTag("dependency") && PROFILE_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER.matches(getCursor())) {
   123	                Xml.Tag tag = getCursor().getValue();
   124	                return matchesGlob(tag.getChildValue("groupId").orElse(null), groupId) &&
   125	                        matchesGlob(tag.getChildValue("artifactId").orElse(null), artifactId);
   126	            }
   127	            return false;
   128	        }
   129	        Xml.Tag tag = getCursor().getValue();
   130	        Map<Scope, List<ResolvedDependency>> dependencies = getResolutionResult().getDependencies();
   131	        for (Scope scope : Scope.values()) {
   132	            if (dependencies.containsKey(scope)) {
   133	                for (ResolvedDependency resolvedDependency : dependencies.get(scope)) {
   134	                    if (matchesGlob(resolvedDependency.getGroupId(), groupId) && matchesGlob(resolvedDependency.getArtifactId(), artifactId)) {
   135	                        String scopeName = tag.getChildValue("scope").orElse(null);
   136	                        Scope tagScope = scopeName != null ? Scope.fromName(scopeName) : null;
   137	                        if (tagScope == null) {
   138	                            tagScope = getResolutionResult().getPom().getManagedScope(
   139	                                    groupId,
   140	                                    artifactId,
   141	                                    tag.getChildValue("type").orElse(null),
   142	                                    tag.getChildValue("classifier").orElse(null)
   143	                            );
   144	                            if (tagScope == null) {
   145	                                tagScope = Scope.Compile;
   146	                            }
   147	                        }
   148	                        Dependency req = resolvedDependency.getRequested();
   149	                        String reqGroup = req.getGroupId();
   150	                        if ((reqGroup == null || reqGroup.equals(tag.getChildValue("groupId").orElse(null))) &&
   151	                                req.getArtifactId().equals(tag.getChildValue("artifactId").orElse(null)) &&
   152	                                scope == tagScope) {
   153	                            return true;
   154	                        }
   155	                    }
   156	                }
   157	            }
   158	        }
   159	        return false;
   160	    }

    16	package org.openrewrite.maven;
    17	
    18	import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
    19	import lombok.Value;
    20	import org.jspecify.annotations.Nullable;
    21	import org.openrewrite.ExecutionContext;
    22	import org.openrewrite.Option;
    23	import org.openrewrite.Recipe;
    24	import org.openrewrite.TreeVisitor;
    25	import org.openrewrite.marker.GitProvenance;
    26	import org.openrewrite.xml.AddToTagVisitor;
    27	import org.openrewrite.xml.ChangeTagValueVisitor;
    28	import org.openrewrite.xml.tree.Xml;
    29	
    30	import java.util.Objects;
    31	import java.util.Optional;
    32	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    33	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    34	
    35	import static org.openrewrite.internal.StringUtils.isNullOrEmpty;
    36	
    37	@Value
    38	@EqualsAndHashCode(callSuper = false)
    39	public class UpdateScmFromGitOrigin extends Recipe {
    40	
    41	    @Option(displayName = "Add if missing",
    42	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will add a `<scm>` section if it is missing. " +
    43	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will only update existing `<scm>` sections.",
    44	            required = false)
    45	    @Nullable
    46	    Boolean addIfMissing;
    47	
    48	    String displayName = "Update SCM with Git origin";
    49	
    50	    String description = "Updates or adds the Maven `<scm>` tag based on the Git remote origin. " +
    51	               "By default, only existing Source Control Management (SCM) sections are updated. Set `addIfMissing` to `true` to also add missing SCM sections.";
    52	
    53	    @Override
    54	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
    55	        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
    56	
    57	            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
    58	            GitOrigin gitOrigin;
    59	
    60	            @Override
    61	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    62	                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
    63	                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
    64	                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
    65	                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
    66	                    return document;
    67	                }
    68	                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();
    69	
    70	                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
    71	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing)) {
    72	                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
    73	                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
    74	                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
    75	                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
    76	                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
    77	                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
    78	                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
    79	                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
    80	                                "</scm>";
    81	                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
    82	                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
    83	                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));
    84	
    85	                    }
    86	                    return document;
    87	                }
    88	
    89	                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
    90	            }
    91	
    92	            @Override
    93	            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    94	                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
    95	                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
    96	                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
    97	                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
    98	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
    99	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
   100	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
   101	                }
   102	                return tag;
   103	            }
   104	
   105	            private Xml.Tag updateScmTag(Xml.Tag tag, String tagName, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   106	                Optional<Xml.Tag> maybeChild = tag.getChild(tagName);
   107	                if (maybeChild.isPresent()) {
   108	                    Xml.Tag childTag = maybeChild.get();
   109	                    String originalUrl = childTag.getValue().orElse("");
   110	                    String updatedUrl = gitOrigin.replaceHostAndPath(originalUrl);
   111	                    if (!originalUrl.equals(updatedUrl)) {
   112	                        tag = (Xml.Tag) new ChangeTagValueVisitor<>(childTag, updatedUrl)
   113	                                .visitNonNull(tag, ctx, getCursor().getParentTreeCursor());
   114	                    }
   115	                }
   116	                return tag;
   117	            }
   118	        };
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    @Value
   122	    static class GitOrigin {
   123	        private static final Pattern[] URL_PATTERNS = {
   124	                // SSH format: git@host:path(.git)?
   125	                Pattern.compile("^git@([^:]+):(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   126	
   127	                // HTTP/HTTPS with optional username and port: http(s)://[username@]host[:port]/path(.git)?
   128	                Pattern.compile("^https?://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   129	
   130	                // SSH with protocol and port: ssh://git@host[:port]/path(.git)?
   131	                Pattern.compile("^ssh://git@([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$"),
   132	
   133	                // Generic protocol://[user@]host[:port]/path(.git)? - catches any other protocols
   134	                Pattern.compile("^[a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://(?:[^@]+@)?([^/:]+(?::[0-9]+)?)/(.+?)(?:\\.git)?$")
   135	        };
   136	
   137	        String host;
   138	        String path;
   139	
   140	        static @Nullable GitOrigin parseGitUrl(String gitUrl) {
   141	            if (!isNullOrEmpty(gitUrl)) {
   142	                for (Pattern pattern : URL_PATTERNS) {
   143	                    Matcher matcher = pattern.matcher(gitUrl);
   144	                    if (matcher.matches()) {
   145	                        return new GitOrigin(matcher.group(1), matcher.group(2));
   146	                    }
   147	                }
   148	            }
   149	            return null;
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        String replaceHostAndPath(String originalUrl) {
   153	            if (isNullOrEmpty(originalUrl)) {
   154	                return originalUrl;
   155	            }
   156	
   157	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("scm:git:")) {
   158	                String actualUrl = originalUrl.substring("scm:git:".length());
   159	                return "scm:git:" + replaceHostAndPath(actualUrl);
   160	            }
   161	
   162	            // Handle git@ format (SSH)
   163	            if (originalUrl.startsWith("git@")) {
   164	                // First check if the URL already has the correct host and path
   165	                String expectedPrefix = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   166	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
   167	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, don't modify
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                // Otherwise, replace the host and path
   171	                Matcher gitMatcher = Pattern.compile("^git@[^:]+:(.+?)$").matcher(originalUrl);
   172	                if (gitMatcher.matches()) {
   173	                    String originalFullPath = gitMatcher.group(1);
   174	                    // Check if original path ends with .git
   175	                    boolean hasGitExtension = originalFullPath.endsWith(".git");
   176	
   177	                    // Build new URL
   178	                    String newUrl = "git@" + host + ":" + path;
   179	                    if (hasGitExtension && !path.endsWith(".git")) {
   180	                        newUrl += ".git";
   181	                    }
   182	                    return newUrl;
   183	                }
   184	            }
   185	
   186	            // Handle protocol-based URLs (http, https, ssh, etc.)
   187	            Matcher protocolMatcher = Pattern.compile("^([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z0-9+.-]*://)(?:([^@/]+)@)?([^/]+)(/[^?#]*)?(.*)?$").matcher(originalUrl);
   188	            if (protocolMatcher.find()) {
   189	                String protocol = protocolMatcher.group(1);
   190	                String user = protocolMatcher.group(2);
   191	                String originalHost = protocolMatcher.group(3);
   192	                String originalPath = protocolMatcher.group(4);
   193	                String suffix = protocolMatcher.group(5) != null ? protocolMatcher.group(5) : "";
   194	
   195	                String userPrefix = (user != null) ? user + "@" : "";
   196	
   197	                // Determine if we need to add .git extension
   198	                boolean needsGitExtension = originalPath != null && originalPath.endsWith(".git") && !path.endsWith(".git");
   199	                String newPath = "/" + path + (needsGitExtension ? ".git" : "");
   200	
   201	                // Check if the base URL already matches (to preserve suffixes)
   202	                String newBaseUrl = protocol + userPrefix + host + newPath;
   203	                if (originalUrl.startsWith(newBaseUrl)) {
   204	                    return originalUrl; // Already correct, preserve any suffix
   205	                }
   206	
   207	                return newBaseUrl + suffix;
   208	            }
   209	
   210	            // Return the original URL if no patterns matched
   211	            return originalUrl;
   212	        }
   213	    }

   195	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getScanner(Scanned acc) {
   196	        return Preconditions.check(acc.usingType || (!StringUtils.isNullOrEmpty(onlyIfUsing) && onlyIfUsing.contains(":")), new MavenIsoVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
   197	            @Override
   198	            public Xml.Document visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   199	                document.getMarkers().findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class).ifPresent(mavenResolutionResult -> {
   200	                    if (mavenResolutionResult.getParent() == null) {
   201	                        acc.rootPoms.add(document);
   202	                    }
   203	                });
   204	                if (acc.usingType) {
   205	                    return document;
   206	                }
   207	                super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   208	                return document;
   209	            }
   210	
   211	            @Override
   212	            public Xml.Tag visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   213	                Xml.Tag t = super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
   214	
   215	                if (isDependencyTag()) {
   216	                    ResolvedDependency dependency = findDependency(t, null);
   217	                    if (dependency != null) {
   218	                        String[] ga = requireNonNull(onlyIfUsing).split(":");
   219	                        ResolvedDependency match = dependency.findDependency(ga[0], ga[1]);
   220	                        if (match != null) {
   221	                            acc.usingType = true;
   222	                        }
   223	                    }
   224	                }
   225	
   226	                return t;
   227	            }
   228	        });
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    @Override
   232	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor(Scanned acc) {
   233	        return Preconditions.check(acc.usingType, new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
   234	            @Override
   235	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   236	                Xml maven = super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   237	
   238	                if (!Boolean.TRUE.equals(addToRootPom) || acc.rootPoms.contains(document)) {
   239	                    ResolvedPom pom = getResolutionResult().getPom();
   240	                    String convertedVersion = pom.getValue(version);
   241	                    if (convertedVersion == null) {
   242	                        return maven;
   243	                    }
   244	                    String convertedGroup = requireNonNull(pom.getValue(groupId));
   245	                    String convertedArtifact = requireNonNull(pom.getValue(artifactId));
   246	                    Validated<VersionComparator> versionValidation = Semver.validate(convertedVersion, versionPattern);
   247	                    if (versionValidation.isValid()) {
   248	                        VersionComparator versionComparator = requireNonNull(versionValidation.getValue());
   249	                        try {
   250	                            // The version of the dependency currently in use (if any) might influence the version comparator
   251	                            // For example, "latest.patch" gives very different results depending on the version in use
   252	                            String currentVersion = getResolutionResult().findDependencies(convertedGroup, convertedArtifact, Scope.fromName(scope)).stream()
   253	                                    .map(ResolvedDependency::getVersion)
   254	                                    .findFirst()
   255	                                    .orElse(existingManagedDependencyVersion());
   256	                            String versionToUse = MavenDependency.findNewerVersion(convertedGroup, convertedArtifact, currentVersion, getResolutionResult(), metadataFailures, versionComparator, ctx);
   257	
   258	                            // Prevent downgrades
   259	                            if (currentVersion != null && versionToUse != null &&
   260	                                    versionComparator.compare(null, currentVersion, versionToUse) >= 0) {
   261	                                return maven;
   262	                            }
   263	
   264	                            if (versionToUse != null && !versionToUse.equals(pom.getValue(existingManagedDependencyVersion()))) {
   265	                                if (ResolvedPom.placeholderHelper.hasPlaceholders(version) && Objects.equals(convertedVersion, versionToUse)) {
   266	                                    // revert back to the original version if the version has a placeholder
   267	                                    versionToUse = version;
   268	                                }
   269	                                doAfterVisit(new AddManagedDependencyVisitor(groupId, artifactId,
   270	                                        versionToUse, scope, type, classifier, because));
   271	                                maybeUpdateModel();
   272	                            }
   273	                        } catch (MavenDownloadingException e) {
   274	                            return e.warn(document);
   275	                        }
   276	                    }
   277	                }
   278	
   279	                return maven;
   280	            }

    60	    List<MavenResolutionResult> modules;
    61	
    62	    @Nullable
    63	    @With
    64	    MavenResolutionResult parent;
    65	
    66	    @With
    67	    Map<Scope, List<ResolvedDependency>> dependencies;
    68	
    69	    @With
    70	    @Nullable
    71	    MavenSettings mavenSettings;
    72	
    73	    @With
    74	    List<String> activeProfiles;
    75	
    76	    @With
    77	    Map<String, String> userProperties;
    78	
    79	    public List<String> getActiveProfiles() {
    80	        // for backwards compatibility with ASTs that were serialized before activeProfiles was added
    81	        //noinspection ConstantValue
    82	        return activeProfiles == null ? emptyList() : activeProfiles;
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    public Map<String, String> getUserProperties() {
    86	        // for backwards compatibility with ASTs that were serialized before userProperties was added
    87	        //noinspection ConstantValue
    88	        return userProperties == null ? emptyMap() : userProperties;
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    public MavenResolutionResult unsafeSetManagedReference(Integer id) {
    92	        this.managedReference = id;
    93	        return this;
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    public @Nullable ResolvedDependency getResolvedDependency(Dependency dependency) {
    97	        for (int i = Scope.values().length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    98	            Scope scope = Scope.values()[i];
    99	            if (dependencies.containsKey(scope)) {
   100	                for (ResolvedDependency resolvedDependency : dependencies.get(scope)) {
   101	                    if (resolvedDependency.getRequested() == dependency) {
   102	                        return resolvedDependency;
   103	                    }
   104	                }
   105	            }
   106	        }
   107	        return null;
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    /**
   111	     * Finds dependencies (including any transitive dependencies) in the model that match the provided group and
   112	     * artifact ids. The search can optionally be limited to a given scope.
   113	     * <p>
   114	     * Note: It is possible for the same dependency to be returned multiple times if it is present in multiple scopes.
   115	     *
   116	     * @param groupId    The groupId as a glob expression
   117	     * @param artifactId The artifactId as a glob expression
   118	     * @param scope      The scope to limit the search to, or null to search all scopes
   119	     * @return A list of matching dependencies
   120	     */
   121	    public List<ResolvedDependency> findDependencies(String groupId, String artifactId, @Nullable Scope scope) {
   122	        return findDependencies(d -> matchesGlob(d.getGroupId(), groupId) && matchesGlob(d.getArtifactId(), artifactId), scope);
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    /**
   126	     * Finds dependencies (including any transitive dependencies) in the model that match the predicate. The search can
   127	     * optionally be limited to a given scope.
   128	     * <p>
   129	     * Note: It is possible for the same dependency to be returned multiple times if it is present in multiple scopes.
   130	     *
   131	     * @param matcher The predicate to match the dependency
   132	     * @param scope   A scope to limit the search to, or null to search all scopes
   133	     * @return A list of matching dependencies
   134	     */
   135	    public List<ResolvedDependency> findDependencies(Predicate<ResolvedDependency> matcher, @Nullable Scope scope) {
   136	        List<ResolvedDependency> found = null;
   137	        for (Map.Entry<Scope, List<ResolvedDependency>> entry : dependencies.entrySet()) {
   138	            if (scope != null && entry.getKey() != scope) {
   139	                continue;
   140	            }

   153	            List<MavenResolutionResult> modules = new ArrayList<>(0);
   154	            for (SourceFile possibleModule : parsed) {
   155	                if (possibleModule == maven) {
   156	                    continue;
   157	                }
   158	                Optional<MavenResolutionResult> maybeModuleResolutionResult = possibleModule.getMarkers().findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class);
   159	                if (!maybeModuleResolutionResult.isPresent()) {
   160	                    continue;
   161	                }
   162	                MavenResolutionResult moduleResolutionResult = maybeModuleResolutionResult.get();
   163	                Parent parent = moduleResolutionResult.getPom().getRequested().getParent();
   164	                if (parent != null &&
   165	                    resolutionResult.getPom().getGroupId().equals(resolutionResult.getPom().getValue(parent.getGroupId())) &&
   166	                    resolutionResult.getPom().getArtifactId().equals(resolutionResult.getPom().getValue(parent.getArtifactId())) &&
   167	                    Objects.equals(resolutionResult.getPom().getValue(resolutionResult.getPom().getVersion()), resolutionResult.getPom().getValue(parent.getVersion()))) {
   168	                    moduleResolutionResult.unsafeSetParent(resolutionResult);
   169	                    modules.add(moduleResolutionResult);
   170	                }
   171	            }
   172	
   173	            if (!modules.isEmpty()) {
   174	                resolutionResult.unsafeSetModules(modules);
   175	            }
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        return parsed.stream();
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    @Override
   182	    public boolean accept(Path path) {
   183	        return "pom.xml".equals(path.toString()) || path.toString().endsWith(".pom");
   184	    }
   185	
   186	    public static Builder builder() {
   187	        return new Builder();
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    public static class Builder extends Parser.Builder {
   191	        private final Collection<String> activeProfiles = new HashSet<>();
   192	        private final Map<String, String> properties = new HashMap<>();
   193	        private boolean skipDependencyResolution;
   194	
   195	        public Builder() {
   196	            super(Xml.Document.class);
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        public Builder skipDependencyResolution(boolean skip) {
   200	            skipDependencyResolution = skip;
   201	            return this;
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        public Builder activeProfiles(@Nullable String... profiles) {
   205	            //noinspection ConstantConditions
   206	            if (profiles != null) {
   207	                addAll(this.activeProfiles, profiles);
   208	            }
   209	            return this;
   210	        }
   211	
   212	        public Builder property(@Nullable String key, @Nullable String value) {
   213	            //noinspection ConstantConditions
   214	            if (key != null && value != null) {
   215	                this.properties.put(key, value);
   216	            }
   217	            return this;
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        @Override
   221	        public MavenParser build() {
   222	            return new MavenParser(activeProfiles, properties, skipDependencyResolution);
   223	        }
   224	
   225	        @Override
   226	        public String getDslName() {
   227	            return "maven";
   228	        }
   229	    }

public class MavenVisitor<P> extends XmlVisitor<P> {

    static final XPathMatcher DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/dependencies/dependency");
    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/dependencies/dependency");
    static final XPathMatcher PLUGIN_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//plugins/plugin/dependencies/dependency");
    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_PLUGIN_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/build/plugins/plugin/dependencies/dependency");
    static final XPathMatcher MANAGED_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/dependencyManagement/dependencies/dependency");
    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_MANAGED_DEPENDENCY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/dependencyManagement/dependencies/dependency");
    static final XPathMatcher PROPERTY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/properties/*");
    static final XPathMatcher PROFILE_PROPERTY_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/profiles/profile/properties/*");
    static final XPathMatcher PLUGIN_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//plugins/plugin");
    static final XPathMatcher ANNOTATION_PROCESSORS_PATH_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//annotationProcessorPaths/path");
    static final XPathMatcher MANAGED_PLUGIN_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("//pluginManagement/plugins/plugin");
    static final XPathMatcher PARENT_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project/parent");
    static final XPathMatcher PROJECT_MATCHER = new XPathMatcher("/project");

    // there are several implicitly defined version properties that we should never attempt to update
    private static final Set<String> IMPLICITLY_DEFINED_VERSION_PROPERTIES = new HashSet<>(Arrays.asList(
            "${version}",
            "${project.version}",
            "${pom.version}",
            "${project.parent.version}",
            "${revision}",
            "${sha1}",
            "${changelist}"
    ));

    private transient Xml.@Nullable Document document;

    @Nullable
    private transient MavenResolutionResult resolutionResult;

    @Override
    public String getLanguage() {
        return "maven";
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isAcceptable(SourceFile sourceFile, P p) {
        return super.isAcceptable(sourceFile, p) &&
                sourceFile.getMarkers().findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class).isPresent();
    }

    protected MavenResolutionResult getResolutionResult() {
        Iterator<Object> itr = getCursor()
                .getPath(Xml.Document.class::isInstance);
        if (itr.hasNext()) {
            Xml.Document newDocument = (Xml.Document) itr.next();
            if (document != null && document != newDocument) {
                throw new IllegalStateException(
                        "The same MavenVisitor instance has been used on two different XML documents. " +
                                "This violates the Recipe contract that they will return a unique visitor instance every time getVisitor() is called.");
            }
            document = newDocument;
        }
        if (resolutionResult == null) {
            resolutionResult = Optional.ofNullable(document)
                    .map(Xml.Document::getMarkers)
                    .flatMap(markers -> markers.findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class))
                    .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Maven visitors should not be visiting XML documents without a Maven marker"));
        }
        return resolutionResult;
    }

    public boolean isPropertyTag() {
        return PROPERTY_MATCHER.matches(getCursor());
    }

    public boolean isProfilePropertyTag() {
        return PROFILE_PROPERTY_MATCHER.matches(getCursor());
    }

    public boolean isDependencyTag() {
        return isTag("dependency") && DEPENDENCY_MATCHER.matches(getCursor());
    }

     *
     * @param groupId    The group ID glob expression to compare the tag against.
     * @param artifactId The artifact ID glob expression to compare the tag against.
     * @return true if the tag matches.
     */
    public boolean isDependencyTag(String groupId, String artifactId) {

    34	 * section of the POM.
    35	 * <p>
    36	 * All dependencies that match {@link #groupPattern} and {@link #artifactPattern} should be

    91	            @Override

   108	
   109	                Collection<ResolvedDependency> manageableDependencies;

   111	                    ResolvedPom pom = getResolutionResult().getPom();
   112	                    GroupArtifactVersion gav = new GroupArtifactVersion(pom.getGav().getGroupId(), pom.getGav().getArtifactId(), pom.getGav().getVersion());
   113	                    manageableDependencies = rootGavToDependencies.get(gav);
   114	                } else {

   116	                }
   117

   126	                                    (ga, existing) -> existing == null || existing.getVersion().compareTo(rmd.getVersion()) < 0 ?

   147	    private MavenResolutionResult findRootPom(MavenResolutionResult pom) {
   148	        if (pom.getParent() == null) {
   149	            return pom;
   150	        }
   151	        return findRootPom(pom.getParent());
   152	    }
   153	
   154	    private static class RemoveVersionTagVisitor extends MavenIsoVisitor<ExecutionContext> {
   155	        private final String groupPattern;
   156	        private final String artifactPattern;
   157	
   158	        public RemoveVersionTagVisitor(String groupPattern, String artifactPattern) {
   159	            this.groupPattern = groupPattern;
   160	            this.artifactPattern = artifactPattern;
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        @Override
   164	        public Xml.Tag visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   165	            if (isDependencyTag() && isDependencyTag(groupPattern, artifactPattern)) {
   166	                tag.getChild("version").ifPresent(versionTag -> doAfterVisit(new RemoveContentVisitor<>(versionTag, false, true)));
   167	                return tag;
   168	            }
   169	            return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
   170	        }

    26	import org.openrewrite.marker.GitProvenance;
    27	import org.openrewrite.maven.tree.MavenResolutionResult;
    28	import org.openrewrite.xml.AddToTagVisitor;
    29	import org.openrewrite.xml.ChangeTagValueVisitor;
    30	import org.openrewrite.xml.tree.Xml;
    31	
    32	import java.util.Objects;
    33	import java.util.Optional;
    34	import java.util.regex.Matcher;
    35	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    36	
    37	import static org.openrewrite.internal.StringUtils.isNullOrEmpty;
    38	
    39	@Value
    40	@EqualsAndHashCode(callSuper = false)
    41	public class UpdateScmFromGitOrigin extends Recipe {
    42	
    43	    @Option(displayName = "Add if missing",
    44	            description = "If set to `true`, the recipe will add a `<scm>` section if it is missing. " +
    45	                          "If set to `false` (default), the recipe will only update existing `<scm>` sections.",
    46	            required = false)
    47	    @Nullable
    48	    Boolean addIfMissing;
    49	
    50	    @Option(displayName = "Update only root pom",
    51	            description = "If set to `true` and `addIfMissing` is also `true`, the recipe will add a missing `<scm>` section only to root POMs. " +
    52	                          "Existing `<scm>` sections will still be updated in all POMs.",
    53	            required = false)
    54	    @Nullable
    55	    Boolean updateOnlyRootPom;
    56	
    57	    @Deprecated
    58	    public UpdateScmFromGitOrigin(@Nullable Boolean addIfMissing) {
    59	        this(addIfMissing, null);
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    @JsonCreator
    63	    public UpdateScmFromGitOrigin(@Nullable Boolean addIfMissing, @Nullable Boolean updateOnlyRootPom) {
    64	        this.addIfMissing = addIfMissing;
    65	        this.updateOnlyRootPom = updateOnlyRootPom;
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    String displayName = "Update SCM with Git origin";
    69	
    70	    String description = "Updates or adds the Maven `<scm>` tag based on the Git remote origin. " +
    71	               "By default, only existing Source Control Management (SCM) sections are updated. Set `addIfMissing` to `true` to also add missing SCM sections.";
    72	
    73	    @Override
    74	    public TreeVisitor<?, ExecutionContext> getVisitor() {
    75	        return new MavenVisitor<ExecutionContext>() {
    76	
    77	            @SuppressWarnings("NotNullFieldNotInitialized")
    78	            GitOrigin gitOrigin;
    79	
    80	            @Override
    81	            public Xml visitDocument(Xml.Document document, ExecutionContext ctx) {
    82	                Optional<GitOrigin> maybeOrigin = document.getMarkers().findFirst(GitProvenance.class)
    83	                        .map(GitProvenance::getOrigin)
    84	                        .map(GitOrigin::parseGitUrl);
    85	                if(!maybeOrigin.isPresent()) {
    86	                    return document;
    87	                }
    88	                gitOrigin = maybeOrigin.get();
    89	
    90	                if(!document.getRoot().getChild("scm").isPresent()) {
    91	                    if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(addIfMissing) &&
    92	                        (!Boolean.TRUE.equals(updateOnlyRootPom) || isRootPom(document))) {
    93	                        // Build the SCM tag with all required elements
    94	                        String httpUrl = "https://" + gitOrigin.getHost() + "/" + gitOrigin.getPath();
    95	                        String gitPath = gitOrigin.getPath().endsWith(".git") ?
    96	                                gitOrigin.getPath().substring(0, gitOrigin.getPath().length() - 4) : gitOrigin.getPath();
    97	                        String scmContent = "<scm>\n" +
    98	                                "  <url>" + httpUrl + "</url>\n" +
    99	                                "  <connection>scm:git:" + httpUrl + (httpUrl.endsWith(".git") ? "" : ".git") + "</connection>\n" +
   100	                                "  <developerConnection>scm:git:git@" + gitOrigin.getHost() + ":" + gitPath + ".git</developerConnection>\n" +
   101	                                "</scm>";
   102	                        document = (Xml.Document) new AddToTagVisitor<>(document.getRoot(), Xml.Tag.build(scmContent),
   103	                                new MavenTagInsertionComparator(document.getRoot().getChildren()))
   104	                                .visitNonNull(document, ctx, Objects.requireNonNull(getCursor().getParent()));
   105	
   106	                    }
   107	                    return document;
   108	                }
   109	
   110	                return super.visitDocument(document, ctx);
   111	            }
   112	
   113	            private boolean isRootPom(Xml.Document document) {
   114	                return document.getMarkers().findFirst(MavenResolutionResult.class)
   115	                        .map(mavenResolutionResult -> mavenResolutionResult.getParent() == null)
   116	                        .orElse(false);
   117	            }
   118	
   119	            @Override
   120	            public Xml visitTag(Xml.Tag tag, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   121	                if ("project".equals(tag.getName())) {
   122	                    return super.visitTag(tag, ctx);
   123	                } else if ("scm".equals(tag.getName())) {
   124	                    // Update existing tags, preserving their URL structure
   125	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "url", ctx);
   126	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "connection", ctx);
   127	                    tag = updateScmTag(tag, "developerConnection", ctx);
   128	                }
   129	                return tag;
   130	            }
   131	
   132	            private Xml.Tag updateScmTag(Xml.Tag tag, String tagName, ExecutionContext ctx) {
   133	                Optional<Xml.Tag> maybeChild = tag.getChild(tagName);
   134	                if (maybeChild.isPresent()) {
   135	                    Xml.Tag childTag = maybeChild.get();
   136	                    String originalUrl = childTag.getValue().orElse("");
   137	                    String updatedUrl = gitOrigin.replaceHostAndPath(originalUrl);
   138	                    if (!originalUrl.equals(updatedUrl)) {
   139	                        tag = (Xml.Tag) new ChangeTagValueVisitor<>(childTag, updatedUrl)
   140	                                .visitNonNull(tag, ctx, getCursor().getParentTreeCursor());
   141	                    }
   142	                }
   143	                return tag;
   144	            }
   145	        };
